<tr>
<td align="right"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:%E6%95%B8" title="Template:数"><abbr title="查看该模板">查</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:%E6%95%B8" title="Template talk:数"><abbr title="讨论该模板">论</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="编辑该模板">编</abbr></a></li></ul></div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>质数</b>（<span lang="en">Prime number</span>），又称<b>素数</b>，指在大于<a href="/wiki/1" title="1">1</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E6%95%B0" title="自然数">自然数</a>中，除了1和该数自身外，无法被其他自然数<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B4%E9%99%A4" title="整除">整除</a>的数（也可定义为只有1与该数本身两个正因数的数）。大于1的自然数若不是质数，则称之为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%88%E6%95%B8" title="合数">合数</a>（也称为合成数）。例如，<a href="/wiki/5" title="5">5</a>是个质数，因为其正因数只有1与5。7是个质数，因为其正因数只有1与7。而4则是个合数，因为除了1与4外，2也是其正因数。6也是个合数，因为除了1与6外，2与3也是其正因数。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E8%A1%93%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="算术基本定理">算术基本定理</a>确立了质数于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E8%AB%96" title="数论">数论</a>里的核心地位：任何大于1的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B4%E6%95%B8" title="整数">整数</a>均可被表示成一串唯一质数之乘积。为了确保该定理的唯一性，1被定义为不是质数，因为在<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E5%BC%8F%E5%88%86%E8%A7%A3" title="因式分解">因式分解</a>中可以有任意多个1（如3、1×3、1×1×3等都是3的有效因数分解）。
</p><p>古希腊数学家<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97" title="欧几里得">欧几里得</a>于公元前300年前后证明有无限多个质数存在（<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E5%87%A0%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="欧几里得定理">欧几里得定理</a>）。现时人们已发现多种验证质数的方法。其中<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A9%A6%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95" title="试除法">试除法</a>比较简单，但需时较长：设被测试的自然数为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，使用此方法者需逐一测试2与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mi>n</mi>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sqrt{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2a2994734eae382ce30100fb17b9447fd8e99f81" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:3.331ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>之间的整数，确保它们无一能整除<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。对于较大或一些具特别形式（如梅森数）的自然数，人们通常使用较有效率的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%BC%94%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="演算法">演算法</a>测试其是否为质数（例如2<sup>82589933</sup>-1是直至2018年12月为止已知最大的梅森质数<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup>，也是直至2018年12月为止已知最大的质数）。虽然人们仍未发现可以完全区别质数与合数的公式，但已建构了质数的分布模式（亦即质数在<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="大数 (数学)">大数</a>时的统计模式）。19世纪晚期得到证明的<a href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="质数定理">质数定理</a>指出：一个任意自然数n为质数的机率反比于其<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E4%BD%8D" title="数位">数位</a>（或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8D%E6%95%B8" title="对数">对数</a>）。
</p><p>许多有关质数的问题依然未解，如<a href="/wiki/%E5%93%A5%E5%BE%B7%E5%B7%B4%E8%B5%AB%E7%8C%9C%E6%83%B3" title="哥德巴赫猜想">哥德巴赫猜想</a>（每个大于2的偶数可表示成两个素数之和）及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AD%AA%E7%94%9F%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0%E7%8C%9C%E6%83%B3" title="孪生质数猜想">孪生质数猜想</a>（存在无穷多对相差2的质数）。这些问题促进了数论各个分支的发展，主要在于数字的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90%E6%95%B8%E8%AB%96" title="解析数论">解析</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E6%95%B8%E8%AB%96" title="代数数论">代数</a>方面。质数被用于资讯科技里的几个程序中，如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E9%96%8B%E9%87%91%E9%91%B0%E5%8A%A0%E5%AF%86" title="公开金钥加密">公钥加密</a>利用了难以将大数分解成其质因数之类的性质。质数亦在其他数学领域里形成了各种广义化的质数概念，主要出现在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="代数">代数</a>里，如<a href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E5%85%83%E7%B4%A0" title="质元素">质元素</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E7%90%86%E6%83%B3" title="质理想">质理想</a>。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E7.BE.A9.E5.92.8C.E4.BE.8B.E5.AD.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义和例子">定义和例子</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：定义和例子">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E6%95%B8" title="自然数">自然数</a>（如1、2、3、4、5、6等）若恰有两个正<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E6%95%B8" title="因数">因数</a>（1及此数本身），则称之为<b>质数</b><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>。大于1的自然数若不是质数，则称之为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%88%E6%95%B8" title="合数">合数</a>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Prime_rectangles.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="380" data-file-width="450" decoding="async" height="253" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Prime_rectangles.svg/300px-Prime_rectangles.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Prime_rectangles.svg/450px-Prime_rectangles.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Prime_rectangles.svg/600px-Prime_rectangles.svg.png 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Prime_rectangles.svg" title="放大"></a></div>数字12不是质数，因为将12以每4个分成1组，恰可分成3组（也有其他分法）。11则无法分成数量都大于1且都相同的各组，而都会有剩余。因此，11为质数。</div></div></div>
<p>在数字1至6间，数字2、3与5为质数，1、4与6则不是质数。1不是质数，其理由见下文。2是质数，因为只有1与2可整除该数。接下来，3亦为质数，因为1与3可整除3，3除以2会余1。因此，3为质数。不过，4是合数，因为2是另一个（除1与4外）可整除4的数：
</p>
<dl><dd>4 = 2 · 2.</dd></dl>
<p>5又是个质数：数字2、3与4均不能整除5。接下来，6会被2或3整除，因为
</p>
<dl><dd>6 = 2 · 3.</dd></dl>
<p>因此，6不是质数。右图显示12不是质数：<span class="nowrap">12 = 3 · 4</span>。不存在大于2的偶数为质数，因为依据定义，任何此类数字<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>均至少有三个不同的因数，即1、2与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。这意指<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不是质数。因此，「奇质数」系指任何大于2的质数。类似地，当使用一般的十进位制时，所有大于5的质数，其尾数均为1、3、7或9，因为尾数0、2、4、6、8为2的倍数，尾数为0或5的数字为5的倍数。
</p><p>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>为一自然数，则1与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>会整除<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。因此，质数的条件可重新叙述为：一个数字为质数，若该数大于1，且没有
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2,3,\ldots ,n-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2,3,\ldots ,n-1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 2,3,\ldots ,n-1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c528d0df41c074250ce227e56dd37024e9a1e7b4" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:13.935ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>会整除<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。另一种叙述方式为：一数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n&gt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>&gt;</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n&gt;1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n&gt;1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee74e1cc07e7041edf0fcbd4481f5cd32ad17b64" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.656ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>为质数，若不能写成两个整数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的乘积，其中这两数均大于1：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n=a\cdot b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mo>=</mo>

<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n=a\cdot b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle n=a\cdot b}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/083e9fcf193435c0829806a150b537e26641793c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:8.4ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>.</dd></dl>
<p>换句话说，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>为质数，若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>无法分成数量都大于1且都相同的各组。
</p><p>由所有质数组成之集合通常标记为<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><b>P</b></span></span>或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {P} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">P</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {P} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {P} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1053af9e662ceaf56c4455f90e0f67273422eded" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.42ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>前168个质数（所有小于1000的质数）为<a href="/wiki/2" title="2">2</a>, <a href="/wiki/3" title="3">3</a>, <a href="/wiki/5" title="5">5</a>, <a href="/wiki/7" title="7">7</a>, <a href="/wiki/11" <h2><span id=".E7.AE.97.E8.A1.93.E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E5.AE.9A.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="算术基本定理">算术基本定理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：算术基本定理">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E8%A1%93%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="算术基本定理">算术基本定理</a></div>
<p>质数对于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E8%AB%96" title="数论">数论</a>与一般数学的重要性来自于「算术基本定理」。该定理指出，每个大于1的整数均可写成一个以上的质数之乘积，且除了质<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E6%95%B8" title="因数">因数</a>的排序不同外是唯一的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>。质数可被认为是自然数的「基本建材」，例如：
</p>
<dl><dd><table>
<tbody><tr>
<td>23244</td>
<td>= 2 · 2 · 3 · 13 · 149
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td></td>
<td>= 2<sup>2</sup> · 3 · 13 · 149. （2<sup>2</sup>表示2的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9" title="平方">平方</a>或2次方。）
</td></tr></tbody></table></dd></dl>
<p>如同此例一般，相同的因数可能出现多次。一个数n的分解：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n=p_{1}\cdot p_{2}\cdot \ldots \cdot p_{t}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msub>
<mi>p</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>p</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>p</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>t</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n=p_{1}\cdot p_{2}\cdot \ldots \cdot p_{t}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle n=p_{1}\cdot p_{2}\cdot \ldots \cdot p_{t}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7e9837aa8f013e230555eaf941d5ba8b7e46d69b" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:18.696ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>成（有限多个）质因数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p_{1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>p</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p_{1}}</annotation>
</semantics>

<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的「因数分解」。算术基本定理可以重新叙述为，任一质数分解除了因数的排序外，都是唯一的。因此，尽管实务上存在许多质数分解演算法来分解较大的数字，但最后都会得到相同的结果。
</p><p>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id="1.E6.98.AF.E5.90.A6.E7.82.BA.E8.B3.AA.E6.95.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1是否为质数">1是否为质数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：1是否为质数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>最早期的希腊人甚至不将1视为是一个数字<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup>，因此不会认为1是质数。到了中世纪与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%87%E8%97%9D%E5%BE%A9%E8%88%88%E6%99%82%E6%9C%9F" title="文艺复兴时期">文艺复兴时期</a>，许多数学家将1纳入作为第一个质数<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-6">[6]</a></sup>。到18世纪中期，<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E9%87%8C%E6%96%AF%E8%92%82%E5%AE%89%C2%B7%E5%93%A5%E5%BE%B7%E5%B7%B4%E8%B5%AB" title="克里斯蒂安·哥德巴赫">克里斯蒂安·哥德巴赫</a>在他与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9D%8E%E6%98%82%E5%93%88%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89" title="李昂哈德·欧拉">李昂哈德·欧拉</a>着名的通信里将1列为第一个质数，但欧拉不同意<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup>。然而，到了19世纪，仍有许多数学家认为数字1是个质数。例如，德里克·诺曼·雷默（Derrick Norman Lehmer）在他那最大达10,006,721的质数列表<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>中，将1列为第1个质数<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup>。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%98%82%E5%88%A9%C2%B7%E5%8B%92%E8%B2%9D%E6%A0%BC" title="昂利·勒贝格">昂利·勒贝格</a>据说是最后一个称1为质数的职业数学家<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup>。到了20世纪初，数学家开始认为1不是个质数，但反而作为「单位」此一特殊类别<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_6-1"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-6">[6]</a></sup>。
</p><p>许多数学成果在称1为质数时，仍将有效，但欧几里何的算术基本定理（如上所述）则无法不重新叙述而仍然成立。例如，数字15可分解成<span class="nowrap">3 · 5</span>及<span class="nowrap"> 1 · 3 · 5</span>；若1被允许为一个质数，则这两个表示法将会被认为是将15分解至质数的不同方法，使得此一定理的陈述必须被修正。同样地，若将1视为质数，<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%83%E6%8B%89%E6%89%98%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%B0%BC%E7%AD%9B%E6%B3%95" title="埃拉托斯特尼筛法">埃拉托斯特尼筛法</a>将无法正常运作：若将1视为质数，此一筛法将会排除掉所有1的倍数（即所有其他的数），只留下数字1。此外，质数有几个1所没有的性质，如欧拉函数的对应值，以及<a href="/wiki/%E9%99%A4%E6%95%B8%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="除数函数">除数函数</a>的总和<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.AD.B7.E5.8F.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="历史">历史</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：历史">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="369" data-file-width="445" decoding="async" height="182" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif/220px-Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif/330px-Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif/440px-Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sieve_of_Eratosthenes_animation.gif" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%83%E6%8B%89%E6%89%98%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%B0%BC%E7%AD%9B%E6%B3%95" title="埃拉托斯特尼筛法">埃拉托斯特尼筛法</a>是个找出在一特定整数以下的所有质数之简单<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%BC%94%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="演算法">演算法</a>，由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98" title="古希腊">古希腊</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6" title="数学家">数学家</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%83%E6%8B%89%E6%89%98%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%B0%BC" title="埃拉托斯特尼">埃拉托斯特尼</a>于公元前3世纪发明。</div></div></div>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%9F%83%E5%8F%8A" title="古埃及">古埃及</a>人的幸存纪录中，有迹象显示他们对质数已有部分认识：例如，在<a href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E5%9B%A0%E5%BE%B7%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E7%BA%B8%E8%8D%89%E4%B9%A6" title="莱因德数学纸草书">莱因德数学纸草书</a>中的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%9F%83%E5%8F%8A%E5%88%86%E6%95%B8" title="古埃及分数">古埃及分数</a>展开时，对质数与对合数有着完全不同的类型。不过，对质数有过具体研究的最早幸存纪录来自<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98" title="古希腊">古希腊</a>。公元前300年左右的《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E5%8E%9F%E6%9C%AC" title="几何原本">几何原本</a>》包含与质数有关的重要定理，如有<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E5%87%A0%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="欧几里得定理">无限多个质数</a>，以及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E8%A1%93%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="算术基本定理">算术基本定理</a>。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97" title="欧几里得">欧几里得</a>亦展示如何从<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A2%85%E6%A3%AE%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0" title="梅森质数">梅森质数</a>建构出<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%85%A8%E6%95%B8" title="完全数">完全数</a>。埃拉托斯特尼提出的埃拉托斯特尼筛法是用来计算质数的一个简单方法，虽然今天使用电脑发现的大质数无法使用这个方法找出。
</p><p>希腊之后，到17世纪之前，质数的研究少有进展。1640年，<a href="/wiki/%E7%9A%AE%E5%9F%83%E7%88%BE%C2%B7%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E8%B2%BB%E9%A6%AC" title="皮埃尔·德·费马">皮埃尔·德·费马</a>叙述了<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B2%BB%E9%A6%AC%E5%B0%8F%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="费马小定理">费马小定理</a>（之后才被<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8" title="莱布尼茨">莱布尼茨</a>与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89" title="欧拉">欧拉</a>证明）。费马亦推测，所有具<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2^{2^{n}}+1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>2</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msup>
<mn>2</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2^{2^{n}}+1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="2^{{2^{n}}}+1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b27f57a4191be088259902a790ef2fb093ffb812" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:7.184ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>形式的数均为质数（称之为<a href="/wiki/%E8%B2%BB%E9%A6%AC%E6%95%B8" title="费马数">费马数</a>），并验证至<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n=4}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>4</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n=4}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n=4" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d928ec15aeef83aade867992ee473933adb6139d" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.656ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>（即2<sup>16</sup> + 1）不过，后来由欧拉发现，下一个费马数2<sup>32</sup> + 1即为合数，且实际上其他已知的费马数都不是质数。法国修道士<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A6%AC%E8%98%AD%C2%B7%E6%A2%85%E6%A3%AE" title="马兰·梅森">马兰·梅森</a>发现有的质数具<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2^{p}-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mn>2</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>p</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2^{p}-1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="2^p-1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d5c5977dbf385ba719fbb90f67b0a3d91e1da6d9" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.224ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>的形式，其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>为质数。为纪念他的贡献，此类质数后来被称为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A2%85%E6%A3%AE%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0" title="梅森质数">梅森质数</a>。
</p><p>欧拉在数论中的成果，许多与质数有关。他证明<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="无穷级数">无穷级数</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{2}}+{\frac {1}{3}}+{\frac {1}{5}}+{\frac {1}{7}}+{\frac {1}{11}}+\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{2}}+{\frac {1}{3}}+{\frac {1}{5}}+{\frac {1}{7}}+{\frac {1}{11}}+\ldots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/598a9d71df993c3e5cb77b1f5083caad06a8c2dc" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:28.081ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span>会<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%BC%E6%95%A3" title="发散">发散</a>。1747年，欧拉证明每个偶<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%85%A8%E6%95%B8" title="完全数">完全数</a>都确实为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2^{p-1}(2^{p}-1)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2^{p-1}(2^{p}-1)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 2^{p-1}(2^{p}-1)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b409475a19a12b9e1dd57930701b1aba02cda461" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:12.356ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>的形式，其中第二个因数为梅森质数。
</p><p>19世纪初，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%8C%E5%AE%89-%E9%A6%AC%E9%87%8C%C2%B7%E5%8B%92%E5%A3%A4%E5%BE%97" title="阿德里安-马里·勒壤得">勒壤得</a>与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF" title="高斯">高斯</a>独立推测，当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%B0%8D%E6%95%B8" title="自然对数">自然对数</a>。黎曼于<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="On the Number of Primes Less Than a Given Magnitude" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="关于小于给定值的质数"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%97%9C%E4%BA%8E%E5%B0%8F%E6%96%BC%E7%B5%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%80%BC%E7%9A%84%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="关于小于给定值的质数（页面不存在）">1859年有关ζ函数的论文</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/On_the_Number_of_Primes_Less_Than_a_Given_Magnitude" title="en:On the Number of Primes Less Than a Given Magnitude"><span dir="auto" lang="en">On the Number of Primes Less Than a Given Magnitude</span></a></span>）</span></span>中勾勒出一个程式，导出了质数定理的证明。其大纲由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%85%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E9%81%94%E9%A6%AC" title="雅克·阿达马">雅克·阿达马</a>与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Charles Jean de la Vallée-Poussin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="查尔斯·贞·德·拉·瓦莱-普森"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9F%A5%E7%88%BE%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E8%B2%9E%C2%B7%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%93%A6%E8%8E%B1-%E6%99%AE%E6%A3%AE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="查尔斯·贞·德·拉·瓦莱-普森（页面不存在）">查尔斯·贞·德·拉·瓦莱-普森</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Jean_de_la_Vall%C3%A9e-Poussin" title="en:Charles Jean de la Vallée-Poussin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Charles Jean de la Vallée-Poussin</span></a></span>）</span></span>所完成，他们于1896年独立证明出<a href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="质数定理">质数定理</a>。
</p><p>证明一个大数是否为质数通常无法由试除法来达成。许多数学家已研究过大数的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E5%88%A4%E5%AE%9A%E6%B3%95%E5%89%87" title="质数判定法则">质数测试</a>，通常局限于特定的数字形式。其中包括费马数的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Pépin's test" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="贝潘测试"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B2%9D%E6%BD%98%E6%B8%AC%E8%A9%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="贝潘测试（页面不存在）">贝潘测试</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/P%C3%A9pin%27s_test" title="en:Pépin's test"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Pépin's test</span></a></span>）</span></span>（1877年）、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%99%AE%E7%BE%85%E7%B5%B2%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="普罗丝定理">普罗丝定理</a>（约1878年）、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A2%E5%8D%A1%E6%96%AF-%E8%8E%B1%E9%BB%98%E6%A3%80%E9%AA%8C%E6%B3%95" title="卢卡斯-莱默检验法">卢卡斯-莱默质数判定法</a>（1856年起）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup>及广义<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lucas primality test" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="卢卡斯质数测试"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9B%A7%E5%8D%A1%E6%96%AF%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E6%B8%AC%E8%A9%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="卢卡斯质数测试（页面不存在）">卢卡斯质数测试</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lucas_primality_test" title="en:Lucas primality test"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lucas primality test</span></a></span>）</span></span>。较近期的演算法，如<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Adleman–Pomerance–Rumely primality test" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="APRT-CL"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=APRT-CL&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="APRT-CL（页面不存在）">APRT-CL</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adleman%E2%80%93Pomerance%E2%80%93Rumely_primality_test" title="en:Adleman–Pomerance–Rumely primality test"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Adleman–Pomerance–Rumely primality test</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Elliptic curve primality" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="椭圆曲线质数证明"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A9%A2%E5%9C%93%E6%9B%B2%E7%B7%9A%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E8%AD%89%E6%98%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="椭圆曲线质数证明（页面不存在）">ECPP</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elliptic_curve_primality" title="en:Elliptic curve primality"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Elliptic curve primality</span></a></span>）</span></span>及<a href="/wiki/AKS%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E6%B8%AC%E8%A9%A6" title="AKS质数测试">AKS</a>等，均可作用于任意数字上，但仍慢上许多。
</p><p>长期以来，质数被认为在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%94%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8" title="纯数学">纯数学</a>以外的地方只有极少数的应用<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>。到了1970年代，发明<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%AF%86%E9%91%B0%E5%8A%A0%E5%AF%86" title="公共密钥加密">公共密钥加密</a>这个概念之后，情况改变了，质数变成了<a href="/wiki/RSA%E5%8A%A0%E5%AF%86%E6%BC%94%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="RSA加密演算法">RSA加密演算法</a>等一阶演算法之基础。
</p><p>自1951年以来，所有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B2%E7%9F%A5%E6%9C%80%E5%A4%A7%E7%9A%84%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8" title="已知最大的质数">已知最大的质数</a>都由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E8%85%A6" title="电脑">电脑</a>所发现。对更大质数的搜寻已在数学界以外的地方产生出兴趣。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A2%85%E6%A3%AE%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0%E5%A4%A7%E6%90%9C%E7%B4%A2" title="互联网梅森质数大搜索">网际网路梅森质数大搜索</a>及其他用来寻找大质数的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%95%A3%E5%BC%8F%E9%81%8B%E7%AE%97" title="分散式运算">分散式运算</a>计画变得流行，在数学家仍持续与质数理论奋斗的同时。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.B4.A0.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E6.95.B0.E7.9B.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="素数的数目">素数的数目</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：素数的数目">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E5%87%A0%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="欧几里得定理">欧几里得定理</a></div>
<p>存在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E7%AA%AE" title="无穷">无限多</a>个质数。另一种说法为，质数序列
</p>
<dl><dd>2, 3, 5, 7, 11, 13, ...</dd></dl>
<p>永远不会结束。此一陈述被称为「欧几里得定理」，以古希腊数学家<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97" title="欧几里得">欧几里得</a>为名，因为他提出了该陈述的第一个证明。已知存在其他更多的证明，包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89" title="欧拉">欧拉</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="数学分析">分析</a>证明、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%93%A5%E5%BE%B7%E5%B7%B4%E8%B5%AB" title="哥德巴赫">哥德巴赫</a>依据<a href="/wiki/%E8%B2%BB%E9%A6%AC%E6%95%B8" title="费马数">费马数</a>的证明<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E5%8B%92%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E5%BC%97%E6%96%AF%E6%BB%95%E4%BC%AF%E6%A0%BC" title="希勒尔·弗斯滕伯格">弗斯滕伯格</a>使用一般<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%92%B2%E5%AD%B8" title="拓扑学">拓扑学</a>的证明<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>，以及<a href="/wiki/%E6%81%A9%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%C2%B7%E5%BA%93%E9%BB%98%E5%B0%94" title="恩斯特·库默尔">库默尔</a>优雅的证明<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.AD.90.E5.B9.BE.E9.87.8C.E5.BE.97.E7.9A.84.E8.AD.89.E6.98.8E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="欧几里得的证明">欧几里得的证明</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：欧几里得的证明">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>欧几里得的证明<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup>取任一个由质数所组成的有限集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。该证明的关键想法为考虑<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>内所有质数相乘后加一的一个数字：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle N=1+\prod _{p\in S}p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>N</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<munder>
<mo>∏<!-- ∏ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>p</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>S</mi>
</mrow>
</munder>
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle N=1+\prod _{p\in S}p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle N=1+\prod _{p\in S}p}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c9743b64c0da36120605e5e039de0395d9e9f73b" style="vertical-align: -3.338ex; width:13.705ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>如同其他自然数一般，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle N}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>N</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle N}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="N" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f5e3890c981ae85503089652feb48b191b57aae3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.064ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>可被至少一个质数整除（即使N本身为质数亦同）。
</p><p>任何可整除N的质数都不可能是有限集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>内的元素（质数），因为后者除N都会余1。所以，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle N}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>N</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle N}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="N" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f5e3890c981ae85503089652feb48b191b57aae3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.064ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>可被其他质数所整除。因此，任一个由质数所组成的有限集合，都可以扩展为更大个由质数所组成之集合。
</p><p>这个证明通常会被错误地描述为，欧几里得一开始假定一个包含所有质数的集合，并导致<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E8%AD%89%E6%B3%95" title="反证法">矛盾</a>；或者是，该集合恰好包含n个最小的质数，而不任意个由质数所组成之集合<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup>。今日，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>个最小质数相乘后加一的一个数字，被称为第<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>个<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E5%B9%BE%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E6%95%B8" title="欧几里得数">欧几里得数</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.AD.90.E6.8B.89.E7.9A.84.E8.A7.A3.E6.9E.90.E8.AD.89.E6.98.8E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="欧拉的解析证明">欧拉的解析证明</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：欧拉的解析证明">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>欧拉的证明使用到质数<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%80%92%E6%95%B8" title="倒数">倒数</a>的总和
</p>

<p>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>够大时，该和会大于任意<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%A6%E6%95%B8" title="实数">实数</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup>。这可证明，存在无限多个质数，否则该和将只会增长至达到最大质数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>是有限的。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.B8.AC.E8.A9.A6.E8.B3.AA.E6.95.B8.E8.88.87.E6.95.B4.E6.95.B8.E5.88.86.E8.A7.A3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="测试质数与整数分解">测试质数与整数分解</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：测试质数与整数分解">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>确认一个数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是否为质数有许多种方法。最基本的程序为试除法，但因为速率很慢，没有什么实际用处。有一类现代的质数测试可适用于任意数字之上，另有一类更有效率的测试方法，则只能适用于特定的数字之上。大多数此类方法只能辨别<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是否为质数。也能给出<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的一个（或全部）质因数之程序称之为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E6%95%B0%E5%88%86%E8%A7%A3" title="因数分解">因数分解</a>演算法。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.A9.A6.E9.99.A4.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="试除法">试除法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：试除法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>测试<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是否为质数的最基本方法为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A9%A6%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95" title="试除法">试除法</a>。此一程序将n除以每个大于1且小于等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="平方根">平方根</a>之整数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>m</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle m}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="m" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a07d98bb302f3856cbabc47b2b9016692e3f7bc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.04ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。若存在一个相除为整数的结果，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不是质数；反之则是个质数。实际上，若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n=ab}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n=ab}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n=a b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0d830d53af96c7ccb02d8922d7abba85022deee4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.721ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是个合数（其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b\neq 1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
<mo>≠<!-- ≠ --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b\neq 1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle b\neq 1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/32a55c3a4b8eca743088b70c7c4d63c773f43c2b" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.258ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>），则其中一个因数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>必定至大为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mi>n</mi>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sqrt{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2a2994734eae382ce30100fb17b9447fd8e99f81" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:3.331ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>。例如，对<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n=37}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mn>37</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>m</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>4</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>5</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>6</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle m=2,3,4,5,6}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle m=2,3,4,5,6}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fe67cf24bcfafab02878bd50fc02688bb3f7689c" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:15.087ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，没有一个数能整除37，因此37为质数。此一程序若能知道直至<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mi>n</mi>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sqrt{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2a2994734eae382ce30100fb17b9447fd8e99f81" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:3.331ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>的所有质数列表，因为试除法只检查<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>m</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle m}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="m" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a07d98bb302f3856cbabc47b2b9016692e3f7bc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.04ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>为质数的状况，所以会更有效率。例如，为检查37是否为质数，只有3个相除是必要的（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m=2,3,5}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>m</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>5</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle m=2,3,5}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle m=2,3,5}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9f6f33cca90d5ed70ff51a17646373abfb8cc7bc" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:10.694ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>），因为4与6为合数。
</p><p>作为一个简单的方法，试除法在测试大整数时很快地会变得不切实际，因为可能的因数数量会随着n的增加而迅速增加。依据下文所述之质数定理，小于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mi>n</mi>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {n}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sqrt{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2a2994734eae382ce30100fb17b9447fd8e99f81" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:3.331ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>的质数之数量约为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\sqrt {n}}{\ln {\sqrt {n}}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<msqrt>
<mi>n</mi>
</msqrt>
<mrow>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mi>n</mi>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {\sqrt {n}}{\ln {\sqrt {n}}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {\sqrt {n}}{\ln {\sqrt {n}}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e2522fae6bd8fcc215fc04dc34ecddc2a3853d4a" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:6.493ex; height:6.843ex;"/></span>，因此使用试除法测试<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是否为质数时，大约会需要用到这么多的数字。对<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n=10^{20}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mn>10</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>20</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n=10^{20}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle n=10^{20}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c7e0d581637cef126cda7049d14112f2840b65c4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:8.694ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>，此一数值约为4.5亿，对许多实际应用而言都太过庞大。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.AF.A9.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="筛法">筛法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：筛法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>一个能给出某个数值以下的所有质数之演算法，称之为质数<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%AF%A9%E8%AB%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="筛论（页面不存在）">筛法</a>，可用于只使用质数的试除法内。最古老的一个例子为<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%83%E6%8B%89%E6%89%98%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%B0%BC%E7%AD%9B%E6%B3%95" title="埃拉托斯特尼筛法">埃拉托斯特尼筛法</a>（见上文），至今仍最常被使用。<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%BF%E7%89%B9%E9%87%91%E7%AF%A9%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="阿特金筛法（页面不存在）">阿特金筛法</a>为另外一例。在电脑出现之前，筛法曾被用来给出10<sup>7</sup>以下的质数列表<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.B3.AA.E6.95.B8.E6.B8.AC.E8.A9.A6.E8.88.87.E8.B3.AA.E6.95.B8.E8.AD.89.E6.98.8E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="质数测试与质数证明">质数测试与质数证明</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%A8%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：质数测试与质数证明">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>现代测试一般的数字<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是否为质数的方法可分成两个主要类型，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9A%A8%E6%A9%9F%E6%BC%94%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="随机演算法">随机</a>（或「蒙特卡洛」）与<a href="/wiki/%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E6%80%A7%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="确定性算法">确定性演算法</a>。确定性演算法可肯定辨别一个数字是否为质数。例如，试除法即是个确定性演算法，因为若正确执行，该方法总是可以辨别一个质数为质数，一个合数为合数。随机演算法一般比较快，但无法完全证明一个数是否为质数。这类测试依靠部分随机的方法来测试一个给定的数字。例如，一测试在应用于质数时总是会通过，但在应用于合数时通过的机率为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>。若重复这个测试<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>次，且每次都通过，则该数为合数的机率为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{(1-p)^{n}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>p</mi>
<msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{(1-p)^{n}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{(1-p)^{n}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9accc582f6b1a85a9484d39ed6b13f3f0724fd71" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:9.036ex; height:6.009ex;"/></span>，会随着测试次数呈指数下滑，因此可越来越确信（虽然总是无法完全确信）该数为质数。另一方面，若测试曾失败过，则可知该数为合数。
</p><p>随机测试的一个特别简单的例子为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B2%BB%E9%A6%AC%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E5%88%A4%E5%AE%9A%E6%B3%95" title="费马质数判定法">费马质数判定法</a>，使用到对任何整数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n^{p}\equiv n(\mod p)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>n</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>p</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>≡<!-- ≡ --></mo>
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mspace width="1em"></mspace>
<mi>mod</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>p</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n^{p}\equiv n(\mod p)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle n^{p}\equiv n(\mod p)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6777f0481633ea97642782a0e3b8063e93a10720" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.801ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>为质数的这个事实（<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B2%BB%E9%A6%AC%E5%B0%8F%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="费马小定理">费马小定理</a>）。若想要测试一个数字<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是否为质数，则可随机选择<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>来计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n^{b}(\mod b)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>n</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mspace width="1em"></mspace>
<mi>mod</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n^{b}(\mod b)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle n^{b}(\mod b)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a75999e1d2fcc3da5e7be870aeb69fd49f4c66ac" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:13.014ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>的值。这个测试的缺点在于，有些合数（<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E9%82%81%E5%85%8B%E7%88%BE%E6%95%B8" title="卡迈克尔数">卡迈克尔数</a>）即使不是质数，也会符合费马恒等式，因此这个测试无法辨别质数与卡迈克尔数，最小的三个卡迈克尔数为561，1105，1729。卡迈克尔数比质数还少上许多，所以这个测试在实际应用上还是有用的。费马质数判定法更强大的延伸方法，包括<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B2%9D%E5%88%A9-PSW%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E6%B8%AC%E8%A9%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="贝利-PSW质数测试（页面不存在）">贝利-PSW</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B1%B3%E5%8B%92-%E6%8B%89%E8%B3%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E5%88%A4%E5%AE%9A%E6%B3%95" title="米勒-拉宾质数判定法">米勒-拉宾</a>与<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Solovay-Strassen%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E6%B8%AC%E8%A9%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Solovay-Strassen质数测试（页面不存在）">Solovay-Strassen质数测试</a>，都保证至少在应用于合数时，有部分时候会失败。
</p><p>确定性演算法不会将合数错误判定为质数。在实务上，最快的此类方法为<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A9%A2%E5%9C%93%E6%9B%B2%E7%B7%9A%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E8%AD%89%E6%98%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="椭圆曲线质数证明（页面不存在）">椭圆曲线质数证明</a>。其运算时间是透过实务分析出来的，不像最新的<a href="/wiki/AKS%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E6%B8%AC%E8%A9%A6" title="AKS质数测试">AKS质数测试</a>，有已被<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E8%AD%89%E6%98%8E" title="数学证明">严格证明</a>出来的<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%A4%8D%E6%9D%82%E5%BA%A6" title="时间复杂度">复杂度</a>。确定性演算法通常较随机演算法来得慢，所以一般会先使用随机演算法，再采用较费时的确定性演算法。
</p><p>下面表格列出一些质数测试。运算时间以被测试的数字<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>来表示，并对随机演算法，以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle k}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>k</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle k}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="k" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>表示其测试次数。此外，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varepsilon }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ε<!-- ε --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varepsilon }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\varepsilon " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a30c89172e5b88edbd45d3e2772c7f5e562e5173" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.083ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是指一任意小的正数，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \log }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>log</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \log }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\log " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/79e4debd0ab1c6ce342d0172a7643733305c37bc" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.972ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>是指一无特定基数的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8D%E6%95%B8" title="对数">对数</a>。<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7O%E7%AC%A6%E5%8F%B7" title="大O符号">大O符号</a>表示，像是在椭圆曲线质数证明里，所需之运算时间最长为一常数（与n无关，但会与ε有关）乘于log<sup>5+ε</sup>(<i>n</i>)。
</p>

</td>
